<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклик.html>о́тклик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótklik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклик.html>о́тклика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклик.html>о́тклики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклик.html>о́ткликов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>echo, repercussion

<li>response

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́звать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отклик.html>о́тклик</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výzvatʹ živój <b>ótklik</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">rose a ready/keen response; evoke a warm response</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(to the password)</i> reply</li>
<li><i>(usually plural)</i> comments; reaction

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:откликаться.html>отклика́ться</a> (9484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откликнуться.html>откли́кнуться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otklíknutʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откликаться.html>отклика́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otklikátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откликнуться.html>откли́кнуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to respond, to answer (to a call, challenge, appeal, etc.)</li>
<li>to respond (with a letter), to comment (in the press)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sound as an answer, to like an echo</li></ol>

***откликнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:откликнуться.html>откли́кнуться</a> (4299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кликнуть.html>кли́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klíknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откликнуться.html>откли́кнуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otklíknutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откликаться.html>отклика́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to respond, to answer (to a call, challenge, appeal, etc.)</li>
<li>to respond (with a letter), to comment (in the press)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sound as an answer, to like an echo</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a> (14007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>клони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otklonítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонять.html>отклоня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deflect</li>
<li>to decline, to turn down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:просьба.html>про́сьбу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otklonítʹ</b> prósʹbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to refuse a request</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поправка.html>попра́вку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otklonítʹ</b> poprávku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to vote down an amendment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приглашение.html>приглаше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otklonítʹ</b> priglašénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to decline an invitation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отклониться.html>отклони́ться</a> (21361)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклониться.html>отклони́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otklonítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклоняться.html>отклоня́ться</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, from something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move to the side, to tilt, to be deflected</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swerve, to deviate</li>
<li>to dodge, to evade</li>
<li>to change the subject</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонять.html>отклоня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otklonjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонить.html>отклони́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deflect</li>
<li>to decline, to turn down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонять.html>отклоня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:просьба.html>про́сьбу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otklonjátʹ</b> prósʹbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to refuse a request</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонять.html>отклоня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поправка.html>попра́вку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otklonjátʹ</b> poprávku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to vote down an amendment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонять.html>отклоня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приглашение.html>приглаше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otklonjátʹ</b> priglašénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to decline an invitation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отклоняться.html>отклоня́ться</a> (22041)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонять.html>отклоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otklonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклоняться.html>отклоня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otklonjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклониться.html>отклони́ться</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, from something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move to the side, to tilt, to be deflected</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swerve, to deviate</li>
<li>to dodge, to evade</li>
<li>to change the subject</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отклонять.html>отклоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otklonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***отключавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отключать.html>отключа́вший</a> (26066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***отключаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отключаться.html>отключа́ться</a> (22944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключать.html>отключа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otključátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключаться.html>отключа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otključátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключиться.html>отключи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become disconnected, to switch off, to shut down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go out <i>(of it)</i>, to conk out, to flake out, to crash out</li>

***отключиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отключиться.html>отключи́ться</a> (12459)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключить.html>отключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключиться.html>отключи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otključítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключаться.html>отключа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become disconnected, to switch off, to shut down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электричество.html>электри́чество</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отключиться.html>отключи́лось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">elektríčestvo <b>otključílosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is [was] a power failure</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go out <i>(of it)</i>, to conk out, to flake out, to crash out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгновенно.html>мгнове́нно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отключиться.html>отключи́ться</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заснуть.html>засну́ть</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mgnovénno <b>otključítʹsja</b> (býstro zasnútʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">go out like a light</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключить.html>отключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключать.html>отключа́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otključátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отключить.html>отключи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-ключи́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">-ključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***откопать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:откопать.html>откопа́ть</a> (16025)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копать.html>копа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откопать.html>откопа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otkopátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откапывать.html>отка́пывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dig out</li>
<li>to exhume, to disinter, to disentomb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dig up, to unearth, to find
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:откопать.html>откопа́ли</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gde vy éto <b>otkopáli</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">where on earth did you dig it up?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***откос.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:откос.html>отко́с</a> (7776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откос.html>отко́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otkós</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откос.html>отко́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откос.html>отко́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откос.html>отко́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slope, slant, scarp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:откос.html>отко́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustítʹ pod <b>otkós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derail, to ditch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:откос.html>отко́с</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">katítʹsja pod <b>otkós</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be on the road to ruin, to get derailed, to go downhill</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:откровенно.html>открове́нно</a> (3652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откровенный.html>открове́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otkrovénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откровенно.html>открове́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otkrovénno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>frankly, candidly, openly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откровенно.html>открове́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otkrovénno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откровенный.html>открове́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otkrovénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откровение.html>открове́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otkrovénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
